Final plan:\n\n1. main(): spawn thread\n2. run(): read, kernelize, choose algorithm, output\n3. kernelize(): degree-0 and degree-1 reduction\n4. solve_nt(): apply NT theorem + solve subproblem\n5. hopcroft_karp(): max bipartite matching\n6. dfs_hk(): DFS for Hopcroft-Karp\n7. konig_cover(): min vertex cover of bipartite graph\n8. bb_solve(): branch and bound on small subgraph\n9. bb_recurse(): recursive B&B\n10. greedy_matching_lb(): lower bound via greedy matching\n11. greedy_vc(): 2-approximation greedy VC\n12. remove_redundant(): remove redundant vertices\n13. greedy_on_active(): greedy VC on active subgraph\n14. remove_redundant_active(): remove redundant in active subgraph\n\nActually wait, I should double-check the soundness of the branching strategy "exclude v (include all neighbors)". \n\nWhen we exclude vertex v from the cover:\n- v is not in cover\n- All edges (v, u) must be covered by u\n- So ALL neighbors of v must be in the cover\n\nThis is different from the standard VC branch which just branches on one edge (u,v): include u OR include v. The "exclude v, include all neighbors" branch is a stronger pruning: if we exclude v, we MUST include all deg(v) neighbors.\n\nFor the first branch (include v): we add v to cover (size +1) and remove v and all its edges.\nFor the second branch (exclude v): we add all deg(v) neighbors to cover (size +deg(v)) and remove v and all those neighbors.\n\nThe branching factor for high-degree vertices is very asymmetric (1 vs. deg). For max-degree vertex with deg=k:\n- Branch 1: add 1 vertex\n- Branch 2: add k vertices\n\nSo the 2-branching on (include v) vs (exclude v → include all neighbors) is useful because the "exclude" branch adds many vertices at once, quickly converging to a solution or pruning.\n\nStandard VC branching analyses show that branching on max-degree vertices gives good performance, especially with the LP lower bound pruning.\n\nAlright, let me write the code. Enough analysis!\n\nHere\'s the complete Rust code:\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::io::{self, Read, Write, BufWriter};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nfn main() {\n    let builder = std::thread::Builder::new().stack_size(256 * 1024 * 1024);\n    let handler = builder.spawn(run).unwrap();\n    handler.join().unwrap();\n}\n\nfn run() {\n    let start = Instant::now();\n    let stdout = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = BufWriter::new(stdout.lock());\n    \n    let mut input = String::new();\n    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut input).unwrap();\n    let mut it = input.split_ascii_whitespace();\n    \n    let n: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n    let m: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n    \n    let mut raw_edges: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::with_capacity(m);\n    for _ in 0..m {\n        let u: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n        let v: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n        if u != v {\n            raw_edges.push((u.min(v), u.max(v)));\n        }\n    }\n    raw_edges.sort_unstable();\n    raw_edges.dedup();\n    \n    if n == 0 || raw_edges.is_empty() {\n        writeln!(out, "0").unwrap();\n        writeln!(out, "").unwrap();\n        return;\n    }\n    \n    let mut adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n];\n    for &(u, v) in &raw_edges {\n        adj[u].push(v);\n        adj[v].push(u);\n    }\n    \n    let mut active = vec![true; n];\n    let mut deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect();\n    let mut in_cover = vec![false; n];\n    \n    // Phase 1: Kernelization\n    kernelize(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut deg, &mut in_cover);\n    \n    // Count kernel size\n    let n_kernel: usize = active.iter().filter(|&&a| a).count();\n    let m_kernel: usize = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).map(|v| deg[v]).sum::<usize>() / 2;\n    \n    if n_kernel == 0 {\n        // Done\n    } else if n_kernel <= 200_000 && m_kernel <= 3_000_000 {\n        // Use NT theorem\n        solve_nt(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut deg, &mut in_cover, &start);\n    } else {\n        // Large: greedy + local search\n        greedy_on_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n        remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n    }\n    \n    let cover: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&i| in_cover[i]).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", cover.len()).unwrap();\n    if cover.is_empty() {\n        writeln!(out, "").unwrap();\n    } else {\n        let s: Vec<String> = cover.iter().map(|x| x.to_string()).collect();\n        writeln!(out, "{}", s.join(" ")).unwrap();\n    }\n}\n\nfn kernelize(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    deg: &mut Vec<usize>,\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut queue: VecDeque<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| deg[v] <= 1).collect();\n    \n    while let Some(v) = queue.pop_front() {\n        if !active[v] { continue; }\n        \n        if deg[v] == 0 {\n            active[v] = false;\n        } else {\n            // deg[v] <= 1, and since it\'s active, must be 1\n            let u_opt = adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied();\n            match u_opt {\n                None => { active[v] = false; }\n                Some(u) => {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    active[u] = false;\n                    active[v] = false;\n                    for &w in &adj[u] {\n                        if active[w] {\n                            deg[w] -= 1;\n                            if deg[w] <= 1 {\n                                queue.push_back(w);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn solve_nt(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    _deg: &mut Vec<usize>,\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    let active_verts: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).collect();\n    let n_a = active_verts.len();\n    if n_a == 0 { return; }\n    \n    let mut to_idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in active_verts.iter().enumerate() {\n        to_idx[v] = i;\n    }\n    \n    // Build bipartite adjacency list\n    // bi_adj[i] = list of right indices connected to left index i\n    let mut bi_adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n_a];\n    for &v in &active_verts {\n        let vi = to_idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if active[u] {\n                let ui = to_idx[u];\n                bi_adj[vi].push(ui);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Run Hopcroft-Karp\n    let (match_l, match_r) = hopcroft_karp(&bi_adj, n_a, n_a);\n    \n    // Find min vertex cover\n    let (cover_l, cover_r) = konig_cover(&bi_adj, n_a, n_a, &match_l, &match_r);\n    \n    // Classify\n    let mut x_half: Vec<usize> = vec![];\n    for (i, &v) in active_verts.iter().enumerate() {\n        match (cover_l[i], cover_r[i]) {\n            (true, true) => {\n                in_cover[v] = true;\n                active[v] = false;\n            }\n            (false, false) => {\n                active[v] = false;\n            }\n            _ => {\n                x_half.push(v);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if x_half.is_empty() { return; }\n    \n    let sub_n = x_half.len();\n    let mut sub_to_idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in x_half.iter().enumerate() {\n        sub_to_idx[v] = i;\n    }\n    \n    let mut sub_adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; sub_n];\n    for &v in &x_half {\n        let vi = sub_to_idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if sub_to_idx[u] != usize::MAX {\n                sub_adj[vi].push(sub_to_idx[u]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let sub_cover = if sub_n <= 500 && start.elapsed().as_millis() < 6000 {\n        bb_solve(sub_n, &sub_adj, start)\n    } else {\n        let mut sc = vec![false; sub_n];\n        greedy_vc(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        remove_redundant(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        sc\n    };\n    \n    for (i, &inc) in sub_cover.iter().enumerate() {\n        if inc {\n            in_cover[x_half[i]] = true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn hopcroft_karp(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    n_left: usize,\n    n_right: usize,\n) -> (Vec<usize>, Vec<usize>) {\n    let nil = n_left;\n    let mut match_l = vec![usize::MAX; n_left];\n    let mut match_r = vec![usize::MAX; n_right];\n    let mut dist = vec![u32::MAX; n_left + 1];\n    \n    loop {\n        // BFS phase\n        let mut queue = VecDeque::new();\n        for u in 0..n_left {\n            if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dist[u] = 0;\n                queue.push_back(u);\n            } else {\n                dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n            }\n        }\n        dist[nil] = u32::MAX;\n        \n        while let Some(u) = queue.pop_front() {\n            if dist[u] < dist[nil] {\n                for &v in &adj[u] {\n                    let w = if match_r[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { match_r[v] };\n                    if dist[w] == u32::MAX {\n                        dist[w] = dist[u] + 1;\n                        if w != nil {\n                            queue.push_back(w);\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        if dist[nil] == u32::MAX { break; }\n        \n        let mut work = vec![0usize; n_left];\n        for u in 0..n_left {\n            if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dfs_hk(u, adj, &mut match_l, &mut match_r, &mut dist, &mut work, nil);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    (match_l, match_r)\n}\n\nfn dfs_hk(\n    u: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    match_l: &mut [usize],\n    match_r: &mut [usize],\n    dist: &mut [u32],\n    work: &mut [usize],\n    nil: usize,\n) -> bool {\n    if u == nil { return true; }\n    while work[u] < adj[u].len() {\n        let v = adj[u][work[u]];\n        let w = if match_r[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { match_r[v] };\n        if dist[w] == dist[u] + 1 && dfs_hk(w, adj, match_l, match_r, dist, work, nil) {\n            match_r[v] = u;\n            match_l[u] = v;\n            return true;\n        }\n        work[u] += 1;\n    }\n    dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n    false\n}\n\nfn konig_cover(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    n_left: usize,\n    n_right: usize,\n    match_l: &[usize],\n    match_r: &[usize],\n) -> (Vec<bool>, Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut in_z_l = vec![false; n_left];\n    let mut in_z_r = vec![false; n_right];\n    let mut queue = VecDeque::new();\n    \n    for u in 0..n_left {\n        if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n            in_z_l[u] = true;\n            queue.push_back(u);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    while let Some(u) = queue.pop_front() {\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !in_z_r[v] {\n                in_z_r[v] = true;\n                if match_r[v] != usize::MAX {\n                    let w = match_r[v];\n                    if !in_z_l[w] {\n                        in_z_l[w] = true;\n                        queue.push_back(w);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let cover_l: Vec<bool> = (0..n_left).map(|u| !in_z_l[u]).collect();\n    let cover_r: Vec<bool> = (0..n_right).map(|v| in_z_r[v]).collect();\n    \n    (cover_l, cover_r)\n}\n\nfn bb_solve(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], start: &Instant) -> Vec<bool> {\n    let mut best = vec![false; n];\n    greedy_vc(n, adj, &mut best);\n    remove_redundant(n, adj, &mut best);\n    let mut best_size: usize = best.iter().filter(|&&b| b).count();\n    \n    let active = vec![true; n];\n    let deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect();\n    let in_cover = vec![false; n];\n    \n    bb_recurse(n, adj, active, deg, in_cover, 0, &mut best_size, &mut best, start);\n    \n    best\n}\n\nfn bb_recurse(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    mut active: Vec<bool>,\n    mut deg: Vec<usize>,\n    mut in_cover: Vec<bool>,\n    current_size: usize,\n    best_size: &mut usize,\n    best: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    if start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8500 { return; }\n    \n    // Apply reduction rules\n    let mut extra = 0usize;\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        \n        for v in 0..n {\n            if !active[v] { continue; }\n            \n            if deg[v] == 0 {\n                active[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            } else if deg[v] == 1 {\n                let u = adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied();\n                match u {\n                    None => {\n                        active[v] = false;\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                    Some(u) => {\n                        in_cover[u] = true;\n                        extra += 1;\n                        active[u] = false;\n                        active[v] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; }\n                        }\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // High-degree rule\n        if *best_size > current_size + extra {\n            let budget = *best_size - current_size - extra - 1;\n            for v in 0..n {\n                if active[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n                    in_cover[v] = true;\n                    extra += 1;\n                    active[v] = false;\n                    for &w in &adj[v] {\n                        if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; }\n                    }\n                    changed = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let new_size = current_size + extra;\n    \n    if new_size >= *best_size { return; }\n    \n    // Lower bound\n    let lb = greedy_matching_lb(n, adj, &active);\n    if new_size + lb >= *best_size { return; }\n    \n    // Find max-degree active vertex\n    let v_opt = (0..n)\n        .filter(|&v| active[v])\n        .max_by_key(|&v| deg[v]);\n    \n    match v_opt {\n        None => {\n            // No active vertices: all edges covered\n            if new_size < *best_size {\n                *best_size = new_size;\n                *best = in_cover.clone();\n            }\n        }\n        Some(v) => {\n            if deg[v] == 0 {\n                // All active vertices are isolated: cover is complete\n                if new_size < *best_size {\n                    *best_size = new_size;\n                    *best = in_cover.clone();\n                }\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            // Branch 1: include v\n            {\n                let mut na = active.clone();\n                let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                let mut nc = in_cover.clone();\n                nc[v] = true;\n                na[v] = false;\n                for &u in &adj[v] {\n                    if na[u] { nd[u] -= 1; }\n                }\n                bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + 1, best_size, best, start);\n            }\n            \n            // Branch 2: exclude v (include all active neighbors)\n            if start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                let neighbors: Vec<usize> = adj[v].iter()\n                    .filter(|&&u| active[u])\n                    .cloned()\n                    .collect();\n                let k = neighbors.len();\n                \n                if new_size + k < *best_size {\n                    let mut na = active.clone();\n                    let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                    let mut nc = in_cover.clone();\n                    \n                    na[v] = false; // v excluded\n                    \n                    for &u in &neighbors {\n                        nc[u] = true;\n                        na[u] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if na[w] { nd[w] -= 1; }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    \n                    bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + k, best_size, best, start);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_matching_lb(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool]) -> usize {\n    let mut matched = vec![false; n];\n    let mut count = 0;\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !matched[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !matched[v] {\n                    matched[u] = true;\n                    matched[v] = true;\n                    count += 1;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    count\n}\n\nfn greedy_vc(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !in_cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if !in_cover[v] {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    in_cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if in_cover[v] && adj[v].iter().all(|&u| in_cover[u]) {\n                in_cover[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_on_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !in_cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !in_cover[v] {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    in_cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant_active(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &[bool],\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && in_cover[v] {\n                let all_covered = adj[v].iter()\n                    .filter(|&&u| active[u])\n                    .all(|&u| in_cover[u]);\n                if all_covered {\n                    in_cover[v] = false;\n                    changed = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWait, there\'s still the issue with the `remove_redundant_active` function. Let V_1 = {v: x*_v = 1}, V_half = {v: x*_v = 1/2}, V_0 = {v: x*_v = 0}\n3. The LP value is |V_1| + |V_half|/2\n4. Let me write it out:\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::io::{self, Read, Write, BufWriter};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nfn main() {\n    let builder = std::thread::Builder::new().stack_size(256 * 1024 * 1024);\n    let handler = builder.spawn(run).unwrap();\n    handler.join().unwrap();\n}\n\nfn run() {\n    let start = Instant::now();\n    let stdout = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = BufWriter::new(stdout.lock());\n    \n    let mut input = String::new();\n    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut input).unwrap();\n    let mut it = input.split_ascii_whitespace();\n    \n    let n: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n    let m: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n    \n    let mut raw_edges: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::with_capacity(m);\n    for _ in 0..m {\n        let u: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n        let v: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n        if u != v {\n            raw_edges.push((u.min(v), u.max(v)));\n        }\n    }\n    raw_edges.sort_unstable();\n    raw_edges.dedup();\n    \n    if n == 0 {\n        writeln!(out, "0").unwrap();\n        writeln!(out, "").unwrap();\n        return;\n    }\n    \n    let mut adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n];\n    for &(u, v) in &raw_edges {\n        adj[u].push(v);\n        adj[v].push(u);\n    }\n    \n    let mut active = vec![true; n];\n    let mut deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect();\n    let mut in_cover = vec![false; n];\n    \n    kernelize(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut deg, &mut in_cover);\n    \n    let n_kernel: usize = active.iter().filter(|&&a| a).count();\n    let m_kernel: usize = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).map(|v| deg[v]).sum::<usize>() / 2;\n    \n    if n_kernel > 0 {\n        if n_kernel <= 200_000 && m_kernel <= 3_000_000 {\n            solve_nt(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut in_cover, &start);\n        } else {\n            greedy_on_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n            remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let cover: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&i| in_cover[i]).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", cover.len()).unwrap();\n    let s: Vec<String> = cover.iter().map(|x| x.to_string()).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", s.join(" ")).unwrap();\n}\n\nfn kernelize(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    deg: &mut Vec<usize>,\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut queue: VecDeque<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| deg[v] <= 1).collect();\n    while let Some(v) = queue.pop_front() {\n        if !active[v] { continue; }\n        if deg[v] == 0 {\n            active[v] = false;\n        } else {\n            // deg[v] must be 1\n            let u_opt = adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied();\n            match u_opt {\n                None => { active[v] = false; }\n                Some(u) => {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    active[u] = false;\n                    active[v] = false;\n                    for &w in &adj[u] {\n                        if active[w] {\n                            deg[w] -= 1;\n                            if deg[w] <= 1 {\n                                queue.push_back(w);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn solve_nt(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    let active_verts: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).collect();\n    let n_a = active_verts.len();\n    if n_a == 0 { return; }\n    \n    let mut to_idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in active_verts.iter().enumerate() {\n        to_idx[v] = i;\n    }\n    \n    let mut bi_adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n_a];\n    for &v in &active_verts {\n        let vi = to_idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if active[u] {\n                bi_adj[vi].push(to_idx[u]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let (match_l, match_r) = hopcroft_karp(&bi_adj, n_a, n_a);\n    let (cover_l, cover_r) = konig_cover(&bi_adj, n_a, n_a, &match_l, &match_r);\n    \n    let mut x_half: Vec<usize> = vec![];\n    for (i, &v) in active_verts.iter().enumerate() {\n        match (cover_l[i], cover_r[i]) {\n            (true, true) => { in_cover[v] = true; active[v] = false; }\n            (false, false) => { active[v] = false; }\n            _ => { x_half.push(v); }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if x_half.is_empty() { return; }\n    \n    let sub_n = x_half.len();\n    let mut sub_to_idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in x_half.iter().enumerate() {\n        sub_to_idx[v] = i;\n    }\n    \n    let mut sub_adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; sub_n];\n    for &v in &x_half {\n        let vi = sub_to_idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if sub_to_idx[u] != usize::MAX {\n                sub_adj[vi].push(sub_to_idx[u]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let sub_cover = if sub_n <= 500 && start.elapsed().as_millis() < 6000 {\n        bb_solve(sub_n, &sub_adj, start)\n    } else {\n        let mut sc = vec![false; sub_n];\n        greedy_vc(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        remove_redundant(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        sc\n    };\n    \n    for (i, &inc) in sub_cover.iter().enumerate() {\n        if inc {\n            in_cover[x_half[i]] = true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn hopcroft_karp(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    n_left: usize,\n    n_right: usize,\n) -> (Vec<usize>, Vec<usize>) {\n    let nil = n_left;\n    let mut match_l = vec![usize::MAX; n_left];\n    let mut match_r = vec![usize::MAX; n_right];\n    let mut dist = vec![u32::MAX; n_left + 1];\n    \n    loop {\n        let mut queue = VecDeque::new();\n        for u in 0..n_left {\n            if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dist[u] = 0;\n                queue.push_back(u);\n            } else {\n                dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n            }\n        }\n        dist[nil] = u32::MAX;\n        \n        while let Some(u) = queue.pop_front() {\n            if dist[u] < dist[nil] {\n                for &v in &adj[u] {\n                    let w = if match_r[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { match_r[v] };\n                    if dist[w] == u32::MAX {\n                        dist[w] = dist[u] + 1;\n                        if w != nil { queue.push_back(w); }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        if dist[nil] == u32::MAX { break; }\n        \n        let mut work = vec![0usize; n_left];\n        for u in 0..n_left {\n            if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dfs_hk(u, adj, &mut match_l, &mut match_r, &mut dist, &mut work, nil);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    (match_l, match_r)\n}\n\nfn dfs_hk(\n    u: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    match_l: &mut [usize],\n    match_r: &mut [usize],\n    dist: &mut [u32],\n    work: &mut [usize],\n    nil: usize,\n) -> bool {\n    if u == nil { return true; }\n    while work[u] < adj[u].len() {\n        let v = adj[u][work[u]];\n        let w = if match_r[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { match_r[v] };\n        if dist[w] == dist[u] + 1 && dfs_hk(w, adj, match_l, match_r, dist, work, nil) {\n            match_r[v] = u;\n            match_l[u] = v;\n            return true;\n        }\n        work[u] += 1;\n    }\n    dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n    false\n}\n\nfn konig_cover(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    n_left: usize,\n    n_right: usize,\n    match_l: &[usize],\n    match_r: &[usize],\n) -> (Vec<bool>, Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut in_z_l = vec![false; n_left];\n    let mut in_z_r = vec![false; n_right];\n    let mut queue = VecDeque::new();\n    \n    for u in 0..n_left {\n        if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n            in_z_l[u] = true;\n            queue.push_back(u);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    while let Some(u) = queue.pop_front() {\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !in_z_r[v] {\n                in_z_r[v] = true;\n                if match_r[v] != usize::MAX {\n                    let w = match_r[v];\n                    if !in_z_l[w] {\n                        in_z_l[w] = true;\n                        queue.push_back(w);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let cover_l: Vec<bool> = (0..n_left).map(|u| !in_z_l[u]).collect();\n    let cover_r: Vec<bool> = (0..n_right).map(|v| in_z_r[v]).collect();\n    (cover_l, cover_r)\n}\n\nfn bb_solve(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], start: &Instant) -> Vec<bool> {\n    let mut best = vec![false; n];\n    greedy_vc(n, adj, &mut best);\n    remove_redundant(n, adj, &mut best);\n    let mut best_size: usize = best.iter().filter(|&&b| b).count();\n    \n    let active = vec![true; n];\n    let deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect();\n    let in_cover = vec![false; n];\n    \n    bb_recurse(n, adj, active, deg, in_cover, 0, &mut best_size, &mut best, start);\n    best\n}\n\nfn bb_recurse(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    mut active: Vec<bool>,\n    mut deg: Vec<usize>,\n    mut in_cover: Vec<bool>,\n    current_size: usize,\n    best_size: &mut usize,\n    best: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    if start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8500 { return; }\n    \n    let mut extra = 0usize;\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if !active[v] { continue; }\n            if deg[v] == 0 {\n                active[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            } else if deg[v] == 1 {\n                let u_opt = adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied();\n                match u_opt {\n                    None => { active[v] = false; changed = true; }\n                    Some(u) => {\n                        in_cover[u] = true;\n                        extra += 1;\n                        active[u] = false;\n                        active[v] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; }\n                        }\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // High-degree rule\n        let budget = best_size.saturating_sub(current_size + extra + 1);\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n                in_cover[v] = true;\n                extra += 1;\n                active[v] = false;\n                for &w in &adj[v] { if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; } }\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let new_size = current_size + extra;\n    if new_size >= *best_size { return; }\n    \n    let lb = greedy_matching_lb(n, adj, &active);\n    if new_size + lb >= *best_size { return; }\n    \n    let v_opt = (0..n)\n        .filter(|&v| active[v] && deg[v] > 0)\n        .max_by_key(|&v| deg[v]);\n    \n    match v_opt {\n        None => {\n            if new_size < *best_size {\n                *best_size = new_size;\n                *best = in_cover;\n            }\n        }\n        Some(v) => {\n            // Branch 1: include v\n            {\n                let mut na = active.clone();\n                let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                let mut nc = in_cover.clone();\n                nc[v] = true;\n                na[v] = false;\n                for &u in &adj[v] { if na[u] { nd[u] -= 1; } }\n                bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + 1, best_size, best, start);\n            }\n            // Branch 2: exclude v (include all active neighbors)\n            if start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                let neighbors: Vec<usize> = adj[v].iter()\n                    .filter(|&&u| active[u])\n                    .cloned()\n                    .collect();\n                let k = neighbors.len();\n                if new_size + k < *best_size {\n                    let mut na = active.clone();\n                    let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                    let mut nc = in_cover.clone();\n                    na[v] = false;\n                    for &u in &neighbors {\n                        nc[u] = true;\n                        na[u] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] { if na[w] { nd[w] -= 1; } }\n                    }\n                    bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + k, best_size, best, start);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_matching_lb(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool]) -> usize {\n    let mut matched = vec![false; n];\n    let mut count = 0;\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !matched[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !matched[v] {\n                    matched[u] = true;\n                    matched[v] = true;\n                    count += 1;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    count\n}\n\nfn greedy_vc(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !in_cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if !in_cover[v] {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    in_cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if in_cover[v] && adj[v].iter().all(|&u| in_cover[u]) {\n                in_cover[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_on_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !in_cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !in_cover[v] {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    in_cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant_active(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &[bool],\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && in_cover[v] {\n                let all_covered = adj[v].iter()\n                    .filter(|&&u| active[u])\n                    .all(|&u| in_cover[u]);\n                if all_covered {\n                    in_cover[v] = false;\n                    changed = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nLet me check for potential warnings:\n1. The DFS depth in a single DFS call is `dist[nil]` (not `dist[nil]/2`), because we start from a left vertex and alternate: left → right → left → ... → nil. Each step increases the level by 1 in the BFS tree. So the depth is `dist[nil]`.\n\nFor `dist[nil]` up to O(sqrt(n_a)) ≈ 450, with each frame using maybe 200 bytes: 450 * 200 = 90KB. Well within 256MB. ✓\n\nBut wait, `dist[nil]` can be arbitrarily large! In the worst case (e.g., a path graph with n vertices), `dist[nil]` in the last phase can be O(n). Crown decomposition finds a bipartite subgraph and efficiently removes part of it from the problem. It can be implemented in O(n+m) time and provides better kernelization than just degree-1 reduction.\n\nCrown reduction:\n1. Find a maximal matching M in the graph\n2. Let I = vertices not in M (independent set)\n3. Let N(I) = neighbors of I (a subset of matched vertices)\n4. Find a maximum matching between I and N(I) in the bipartite subgraph\n5. If max matching in this bipartite graph = |I|: apply crown reduction\n   - Add N(I) to cover, remove N(I) and I and all incident edges\n6. Else: apply LP lower bound argument\n\nThis is more complex to implement and might not be worth it for this problem.\n\nLet me also consider: for the large graph case, after the greedy matching + redundancy removal, could I apply a few rounds of 2-1 swaps to further improve? Remove u1, u2, add w.\n\nFor one round: O(n + m) to find all such triples. If found, apply, repeat. Let me add a few rounds of this:\n\n```rust\nfn two_one_swap(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    // For each cover vertex u, find non-cover active neighbors\n    // If u has exactly 1 non-cover active neighbor w, record (u, w)\n    let mut unique_partner: Vec<Option<usize>> = vec![None; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !active[u] || !in_cover[u] { continue; }\n        let non_cover: Vec<usize> = adj[u].iter()\n            .filter(|&&v| active[v] && !in_cover[v])\n            .cloned()\n            .collect();\n        if non_cover.len() == 1 {\n            unique_partner[u] = Some(non_cover[0]);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // For each non-cover vertex w, count how many cover vertices have w as their unique partner\n    let mut w_partners: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if let Some(w) = unique_partner[u] {\n            w_partners[w].push(u);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    for w in 0..n {\n        if !active[w] || in_cover[w] { continue; }\n        if w_partners[w].len() >= 2 {\n            // Apply swap: remove w_partners[w][0] and w_partners[w][1], add w\n            in_cover[w_partners[w][0]] = false;\n            in_cover[w_partners[w][1]] = false;\n            in_cover[w] = true;\n            return true; // swap applied\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n```\n\nAnd in the main algorithm:\n```rust\nloop {\n    if !two_one_swap(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover) { break; }\n    remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n    if start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8000 { break; }\n}\n```\n\nThis could significantly improve the solution for many graph structures. }\n            remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAnd implement `two_one_swap_active`:\n\n```rust\nfn two_one_swap_active(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &[bool],\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) -> bool {\n    // For each cover vertex u, count non-cover active neighbors\n    // If exactly 1, record the unique non-cover active neighbor\n    let mut unique_w: Vec<i64> = vec![-1; n]; // -1 = not applicable, >= 0 = unique non-cover neighbor idx\n    \n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !active[u] || !in_cover[u] { continue; }\n        let mut cnt = 0;\n        let mut w_idx = usize::MAX;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if active[v] && !in_cover[v] {\n                cnt += 1;\n                if cnt == 1 { w_idx = v; }\n                else { break; }\n            }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 { unique_w[u] = w_idx as i64; }\n    }\n    \n    // For each non-cover vertex w, collect cover vertices with w as unique partner\n    // We need w to have >= 2 such partners\n    // To avoid O(n^2), group by w\n    let mut w_count: Vec<usize> = vec![0; n];\n    let mut w_first: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut w_second: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    \n    for u in 0..n {\n        if unique_w[u] >= 0 {\n            let w = unique_w[u] as usize;\n            w_count[w] += 1;\n            if w_count[w] == 1 { w_first[w] = u; }\n            else if w_count[w] == 2 { w_second[w] = u; }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    for w in 0..n {\n        if w_count[w] >= 2 {\n            let u1 = w_first[w];\n            let u2 = w_second[w];\n            in_cover[u1] = false;\n            in_cover[u2] = false;\n            in_cover[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    false\n}\n```\n\nThis is O(n + m) per call and correctly identifies 2-1 swap opportunities.\n\nBut wait, there\'s a correctness issue: when we apply the swap (remove u1 and u2, add w), does it maintain a valid vertex cover?\n\n- Edge (u1, w): u1 removed, w added → covered by w ✓\n- Edge (u2, w): u2 removed, w added → covered by w ✓\n- Any other edge incident to u1: since unique_w[u1] == w, u1 has exactly 1 non-cover neighbor (w). So all other active neighbors of u1 are in the cover. After removing u1, these edges are still covered by those neighbors. ✓\n- Any other edge incident to u2: similarly. ✓\n- Any edge incident to w (other than to u1 and u2): before the swap, w is not in cover. These edges must be covered by the other endpoint. After the swap, w is in cover, so these edges are definitely covered. ✓\n\nSo the swap is valid! ✓\n\nAnd the cover size decreases by 1 (remove 2, add 1). ✓\n\nGreat, the swap is correct and beneficial.\n\nFor efficiency: the `w_count`, `w_first`, `w_second` arrays are O(n). The main loop is O(n + m) (iterating over all vertices and their adjacency lists). Total: O(n + m) per call. ✓\n\nNow, one issue: after applying the swap, `unique_w[u1]` and `unique_w[u2]` are computed based on the OLD cover state. After the swap, other cover vertices might have their unique partner changed (e.g., if some vertex u3 had both u1 and w as cover neighbors, and u1\'s edges are now uncovered... wait, u3 is a cover vertex. Its non-cover neighbors include... w was non-cover before, now w is cover. So the set of non-cover neighbors of u3 might change.\n\nBut since we call `two_one_swap_active` and return `true` immediately after the first swap, the arrays are recomputed in the next call. ✓ (We only apply ONE swap per call, then recompute everything.)\n\nThis is correct but might be slow since we recompute O(n + m) work for each swap. For large graphs, this could be a bottleneck. But with the time limit, we\'ll just do as many swaps as possible.\n\nAlternatively, I could apply ALL possible non-overlapping swaps in one pass (batch swapping). But this risks correctness issues if swaps interact. Let me keep the single-swap-per-call approach for safety.\n\nOK I think the algorithm is solid now. Let me write the complete final code, including the two_one_swap.\n\nActually, wait. I want to make sure the output is always valid (all edges covered). Let me add a debug assertion:\n\n```rust\n#[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n{\n    for &(u, v) in &raw_edges {\n        assert!(in_cover[u] || in_cover[v], \n            "Edge ({},{}) not covered!", u, v);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis only runs in debug builds (not release), so it won\'t slow down the actual submission. ✓\n\nActually, for safety in the actual submission, let me not include this assert. If there\'s a bug, the checker will catch it.\n\nOK I realize I\'ve been going back and forth too long. Let me just write the clean final code now, including the two-one swap for large graphs.\n\nHere\'s my final code structure:\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::io::{self, Read, Write, BufWriter};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nfn main() {\n    // Spawn thread with large stack\n    // ...\n}\n\nfn run() {\n    // Read input, build graph, kernelize, choose algorithm, output\n}\n\nfn kernelize(...) { ... }\nfn solve_nt(...) { ... }\nfn hopcroft_karp(...) -> (Vec<usize>, Vec<usize>) { ... }\nfn dfs_hk(...) -> bool { ... }\nfn konig_cover(...) -> (Vec<bool>, Vec<bool>) { ... }\nfn bb_solve(...) -> Vec<bool> { ... }\nfn bb_recurse(...) { ... }\nfn greedy_matching_lb(...) -> usize { ... }\nfn greedy_vc(...) { ... }\nfn remove_redundant(...) { ... }\nfn greedy_on_active(...) { ... }\nfn remove_redundant_active(...) { ... }\nfn two_one_swap_active(...) -> bool { ... }\n```\n\nLet me now write this. I need to be careful to avoid warnings:\n- All function parameters should be used\n- No unused variables\n- No dead code (unless all functions are called)\n\nFor `n_right` in `hopcroft_karp`: used to create `match_r = vec![usize::MAX; n_right]`. ✓\nFor `n_right` in `konig_cover`: used to create `in_z_r = vec![false; n_right]` and `cover_r`. ✓\n\nLet me trace through one more time for potential issues...\n\nIn `solve_nt`, when I build `sub_adj`, I might add the same edge twice (once from each direction). This is fine for an undirected graph representation, but it might cause issues in `remove_redundant` if a vertex has the same neighbor listed twice:\n\nFor `remove_redundant` to work correctly, we check `adj[v].iter().all(|&u| in_cover[u])`. If u appears twice in adj[v], we check `in_cover[u]` twice, which is idempotent. ✓\n\nFor `greedy_vc`, if we find the same v twice in adj[u] and both are not in cover, we add both u and v to cover. Idempotent. ✓\n\nFor `greedy_matching_lb`, duplicates in adj don\'t affect correctness since we check `matched[v]` before matching. ✓\n\nSo duplicates in adj are harmless for correctness but slightly wasteful. Since the original adj was deduplicated, and sub_adj is built from it, sub_adj should also be duplicate-free. ✓ (Because for each u in adj[v], we add it to sub_adj[vi] once. Each u appears at most once in adj[v] since adj is deduplicated.)\n\nOK I\'m convinced. Let me write the final code.\n\nHmm, one concern: in the `bb_recurse`, I\'m cloning vectors inside the branches:\n```rust\nlet mut na = active.clone();\nlet mut nd = deg.clone();\nlet mut nc = in_cover.clone();\n```\n\nFor n = 500 (max for B&B), each Vec<bool> is 500 bytes and Vec<usize> is 4000 bytes. Total per clone set: ~9000 bytes. With recursion depth up to 500 and 2 branches, the memory usage could be:\n- Depth * 2 * 3 * 9KB ≈ 500 * 2 * 27KB = 27MB. This is within the 256MB stack.\n\nActually wait, the clones are on the heap, not the stack. Only the Vec metadata (pointer + length + capacity) is on the stack, which is 24 bytes per Vec. The actual data (up to 4KB per Vec) is on the heap. So stack usage per frame: 3 * 24 = 72 bytes (for the Vec metadata). Total stack: 500 * 72 * 2 = 72KB. Fine. ✓\n\nAnd heap: up to 500 * 2 * 3 * max(4KB, 0.5KB) ≈ 500 * 2 * 12KB = 12MB. Fine. ✓\n\nOK let me write the final code. Here\'s the FINAL version:\n\nActually, I want to double-check: when bb_recurse returns, do we drop all the clones? Let me just write two versions.\n\nOr better: factor out the common logic:\n\n```rust\nfn two_one_swap_generic(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &[bool],\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) -> bool {\n    let mut unique_w: Vec<Option<usize>> = vec![None; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !active[u] || !in_cover[u] { continue; }\n        let mut cnt = 0;\n        let mut w_found = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if active[v] && !in_cover[v] {\n                cnt += 1;\n                w_found = v;\n                if cnt > 1 { break; }\n            }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 { unique_w[u] = Some(w_found); }\n    }\n    \n    let mut w_first = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut w_second = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    \n    for u in 0..n {\n        if let Some(w) = unique_w[u] {\n            if w_first[w] == usize::MAX { w_first[w] = u; }\n            else if w_second[w] == usize::MAX { w_second[w] = u; }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    for w in 0..n {\n        if active[w] && !in_cover[w] && w_second[w] != usize::MAX {\n            in_cover[w_first[w]] = false;\n            in_cover[w_second[w]] = false;\n            in_cover[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n```\n\nI can use this for both cases:\n- For the subgraph: create a fake `active_sub = vec![true; sub_n]` and call `two_one_swap_generic(sub_n, &sub_adj, &active_sub, &mut sc)`\n- For the large active graph: call `two_one_swap_generic(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover)`\n\nBut creating `active_sub = vec![true; sub_n]` is a small allocation. Let me just write both.\n\nOK OK OK. Writing the code now. Final version:\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::io::{self, Read, Write, BufWriter};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nfn main() {\n    let builder = std::thread::Builder::new().stack_size(256 * 1024 * 1024);\n    builder.spawn(run).unwrap().join().unwrap();\n}\n\nfn run() {\n    let start = Instant::now();\n    let stdout = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = BufWriter::new(stdout.lock());\n    \n    let mut input = String::new();\n    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut input).unwrap();\n    let mut it = input.split_ascii_whitespace();\n    \n    let n: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n    let m_in: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n    \n    let mut raw_edges: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::with_capacity(m_in);\n    for _ in 0..m_in {\n        let u: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n        let v: usize = it.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();\n        if u != v {\n            raw_edges.push((u.min(v), u.max(v)));\n        }\n    }\n    raw_edges.sort_unstable();\n    raw_edges.dedup();\n    \n    if n == 0 {\n        writeln!(out, "0").unwrap();\n        writeln!(out, "").unwrap();\n        return;\n    }\n    \n    let mut adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n];\n    for &(u, v) in &raw_edges {\n        adj[u].push(v);\n        adj[v].push(u);\n    }\n    drop(raw_edges); // free memory\n    \n    let mut active = vec![true; n];\n    let mut deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect();\n    let mut in_cover = vec![false; n];\n    \n    kernelize(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut deg, &mut in_cover);\n    \n    let n_kernel: usize = active.iter().filter(|&&a| a).count();\n    let m_kernel: usize = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).map(|v| deg[v]).sum::<usize>() / 2;\n    \n    if n_kernel > 0 {\n        if n_kernel <= 200_000 && m_kernel <= 3_000_000 {\n            solve_nt(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut in_cover, &start);\n        } else {\n            greedy_on_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n            remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n            while start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                if !two_one_swap_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover) { break; }\n                remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut in_cover);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let cover: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&i| in_cover[i]).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", cover.len()).unwrap();\n    let parts: Vec<String> = cover.iter().map(|x| x.to_string()).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", parts.join(" ")).unwrap();\n}\n```\n\nNow all the helper functions. Let me write them all:\n\n```rust\nfn kernelize(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    deg: &mut Vec<usize>,\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut queue: VecDeque<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| deg[v] <= 1).collect();\n    while let Some(v) = queue.pop_front() {\n        if !active[v] { continue; }\n        if deg[v] == 0 {\n            active[v] = false;\n        } else {\n            match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied() {\n                None => { active[v] = false; }\n                Some(u) => {\n                    in_cover[u] = true;\n                    active[u] = false;\n                    active[v] = false;\n                    for &w in &adj[u] {\n                        if active[w] {\n                            deg[w] -= 1;\n                            if deg[w] <= 1 { queue.push_back(w); }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn solve_nt(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    in_cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    let av: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).collect();\n    let na = av.len();\n    if na == 0 { return; }\n    \n    let mut idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in av.iter().enumerate() { idx[v] = i; }\n    \n    // Build bipartite adj (left=av, right=av, symmetric edges for each original edge)\n    let mut bi: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; na];\n    for &v in &av {\n        let vi = idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if active[u] { bi[vi].push(idx[u]); }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let (ml, mr) = hopcroft_karp(&bi, na, na);\n    let (cl, cr) = konig_cover(&bi, na, na, &ml, &mr);\n    \n    let mut xhalf: Vec<usize> = vec![];\n    for (i, &v) in av.iter().enumerate() {\n        match (cl[i], cr[i]) {\n            (true, true) => { in_cover[v] = true; active[v] = false; }\n            (false, false) => { active[v] = false; }\n            _ => { xhalf.push(v); }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if xhalf.is_empty() { return; }\n    \n    let sn = xhalf.len();\n    let mut sidx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in xhalf.iter().enumerate() { sidx[v] = i; }\n    \n    let mut sadj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; sn];\n    for &v in &xhalf {\n        let vi = sidx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if sidx[u] != usize::MAX {\n                sadj[vi].push(sidx[u]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let sc = if sn <= 500 && start.elapsed().as_millis() < 6000 {\n        bb_solve(sn, &sadj, start)\n    } else {\n        let mut sc = vec![false; sn];\n        greedy_vc(sn, &sadj, &mut sc);\n        remove_redundant(sn, &sadj, &mut sc);\n        while start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n            if !two_one_swap(sn, &sadj, &mut sc) { break; }\n            remove_redundant(sn, &sadj, &mut sc);\n        }\n        sc\n    };\n    \n    for (i, &inc) in sc.iter().enumerate() {\n        if inc { in_cover[xhalf[i]] = true; }\n    }\n}\n\nfn hopcroft_karp(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    nl: usize,\n    nr: usize,\n) -> (Vec<usize>, Vec<usize>) {\n    let nil = nl;\n    let mut ml = vec![usize::MAX; nl];\n    let mut mr = vec![usize::MAX; nr];\n    let mut dist = vec![u32::MAX; nl + 1];\n    loop {\n        // BFS\n        let mut q = VecDeque::new();\n        for u in 0..nl {\n            if ml[u] == usize::MAX { dist[u] = 0; q.push_back(u); }\n            else { dist[u] = u32::MAX; }\n        }\n        dist[nil] = u32::MAX;\n        while let Some(u) = q.pop_front() {\n            if dist[u] < dist[nil] {\n                for &v in &adj[u] {\n                    let w = if mr[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { mr[v] };\n                    if dist[w] == u32::MAX {\n                        dist[w] = dist[u] + 1;\n                        if w != nil { q.push_back(w); }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        if dist[nil] == u32::MAX { break; }\n        let mut work = vec![0usize; nl];\n        for u in 0..nl {\n            if ml[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dfs_hk(u, adj, &mut ml, &mut mr, &mut dist, &mut work, nil);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    (ml, mr)\n}\n\nfn dfs_hk(\n    u: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    ml: &mut [usize], mr: &mut [usize],\n    dist: &mut [u32], work: &mut [usize], nil: usize,\n) -> bool {\n    if u == nil { return true; }\n    while work[u] < adj[u].len() {\n        let v = adj[u][work[u]];\n        let w = if mr[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { mr[v] };\n        if dist[w] == dist[u] + 1 && dfs_hk(w, adj, ml, mr, dist, work, nil) {\n            mr[v] = u; ml[u] = v; return true;\n        }\n        work[u] += 1;\n    }\n    dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n    false\n}\n\nfn konig_cover(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>], nl: usize, nr: usize,\n    ml: &[usize], mr: &[usize],\n) -> (Vec<bool>, Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut zl = vec![false; nl];\n    let mut zr = vec![false; nr];\n    let mut q = VecDeque::new();\n    for u in 0..nl {\n        if ml[u] == usize::MAX { zl[u] = true; q.push_back(u); }\n    }\n    while let Some(u) = q.pop_front() {\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !zr[v] {\n                zr[v] = true;\n                if mr[v] != usize::MAX && !zl[mr[v]] {\n                    zl[mr[v]] = true;\n                    q.push_back(mr[v]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    let cl: Vec<bool> = (0..nl).map(|u| !zl[u]).collect();\n    let cr: Vec<bool> = (0..nr).map(|v| zr[v]).collect();\n    (cl, cr)\n}\n\nfn bb_solve(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], start: &Instant) -> Vec<bool> {\n    let mut best = vec![false; n];\n    greedy_vc(n, adj, &mut best);\n    remove_redundant(n, adj, &mut best);\n    let mut bs = best.iter().filter(|&&b| b).count();\n    bb_recurse(n, adj, vec![true; n],\n        (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect(),\n        vec![false; n], 0, &mut bs, &mut best, start);\n    best\n}\n\nfn bb_recurse(\n    n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    mut active: Vec<bool>, mut deg: Vec<usize>, mut cov: Vec<bool>,\n    cur: usize, best_sz: &mut usize, best: &mut Vec<bool>, start: &Instant,\n) {\n    if start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8500 { return; }\n    \n    let mut extra = 0usize;\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if !active[v] { continue; }\n            if deg[v] == 0 {\n                active[v] = false; changed = true;\n            } else if deg[v] == 1 {\n                match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied() {\n                    None => { active[v] = false; changed = true; }\n                    Some(u) => {\n                        cov[u] = true; extra += 1;\n                        active[u] = false; active[v] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; }\n                        }\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        let budget = best_sz.saturating_sub(cur + extra + 1);\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n                cov[v] = true; extra += 1;\n                active[v] = false;\n                for &w in &adj[v] { if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; } }\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let nsz = cur + extra;\n    if nsz >= *best_sz { return; }\n    let lb = greedy_lb(n, adj, &active);\n    if nsz + lb >= *best_sz { return; }\n    \n    let vopt = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v] && deg[v] > 0).max_by_key(|&v| deg[v]);\n    match vopt {\n        None => { *best_sz = nsz; *best = cov; }\n        Some(v) => {\n            // Include v\n            {\n                let mut na = active.clone();\n                let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                nc[v] = true; na[v] = false;\n                for &u in &adj[v] { if na[u] { nd[u] -= 1; } }\n                bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, nsz+1, best_sz, best, start);\n            }\n            // Exclude v (include all active neighbors)\n            if start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                let nbrs: Vec<usize> = adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| active[u]).cloned().collect();\n                let k = nbrs.len();\n                if nsz + k < *best_sz {\n                    let mut na = active.clone();\n                    let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                    let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                    na[v] = false;\n                    for &u in &nbrs {\n                        nc[u] = true; na[u] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] { if na[w] { nd[w] -= 1; } }\n                    }\n                    bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, nsz+k, best_sz, best, start);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_lb(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool]) -> usize {\n    let mut matched = vec![false; n];\n    let mut cnt = 0;\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !matched[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !matched[v] {\n                    matched[u] = true; matched[v] = true; cnt += 1; break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    cnt\n}\n\nfn greedy_vc(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cov[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if !cov[v] { cov[u] = true; cov[v] = true; break; }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut ch = true;\n    while ch {\n        ch = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if cov[v] && adj[v].iter().all(|&u| cov[u]) {\n                cov[v] = false; ch = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_on_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !cov[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !cov[v] { cov[u] = true; cov[v] = true; break; }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut ch = true;\n    while ch {\n        ch = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && cov[v] {\n                if adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| active[u]).all(|&u| cov[u]) {\n                    cov[v] = false; ch = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn two_one_swap(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut uniq_w: Vec<Option<usize>> = vec![None; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cov[u] { continue; }\n        let mut cnt = 0;\n        let mut w = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !cov[v] { cnt += 1; w = v; if cnt > 1 { break; } }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 { uniq_w[u] = Some(w); }\n    }\n    let mut wf = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut ws = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if let Some(w) = uniq_w[u] {\n            if wf[w] == usize::MAX { wf[w] = u; }\n            else if ws[w] == usize::MAX { ws[w] = u; }\n        }\n    }\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if !cov[w] && ws[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cov[wf[w]] = false; cov[ws[w]] = false; cov[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n\nfn two_one_swap_active(\n    n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cov: &mut Vec<bool>\n) -> bool {\n    let mut uniq_w: Vec<Option<usize>> = vec![None; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !active[u] || !cov[u] { continue; }\n        let mut cnt = 0;\n        let mut w = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if active[v] && !cov[v] { cnt += 1; w = v; if cnt > 1 { break; } }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 { uniq_w[u] = Some(w); }\n    }\n    let mut wf = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut ws = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if let Some(w) = uniq_w[u] {\n            if wf[w] == usize::MAX { wf[w] = u; }\n            else if ws[w] == usize::MAX { ws[w] = u; }\n        }\n    }\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if active[w] && !cov[w] && ws[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cov[wf[w]] = false; cov[ws[w]] = false; cov[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n```\n\nOK I think this is the complete code. No cycling possible since cover size strictly decreases. ✓\n\n8. Memory for BB: I mentioned that active.clone(), deg.clone(), cov.clone() are on the heap. Hopcroft-Karp\'s BFS and DFS involve traversing adjacency lists which is cache-unfriendly for large graphs.
