Let me use m_kernel <= 500K:\n- bipartite m = 1M: 447 * 1M = 447M ops → 2.2 seconds. OK.\n\nAnd for very small graphs (n_kernel <= 10K), even large m is fine:\n```rust\nif (n_kernel <= 10_000) || (n_kernel <= 200_000 && m_kernel <= 500_000) {\n    solve_nt(...);\n}\n```\n\nThis is getting complicated. Let me just use one threshold: n_kernel <= 100K AND m_kernel <= 1M. This is conservative and should work within the time limit for most cases.\n\nFor graphs with n_kernel > 100K or m_kernel > 1M, we use greedy + swaps. The 2-approximation from greedy is acceptable for large instances.\n\nAlternatively, I could time the Hopcroft-Karp and fall back to greedy if it\'s taking too long. But that\'s more complex to implement.\n\nLet me just go with n_kernel <= 100K AND m_kernel <= 1.5M.\n\nOK enough agonizing. Let me write the final code with these settings and submit it.\n\nWait, one more consideration: the machine has 64 cores. Could I parallelize the algorithm? In Rust, I could use Rayon for parallel iterators. But implementing parallel Hopcroft-Karp or parallel B&B is non-trivial and risky for correctness. Let me stick with single-threaded for safety.\n\nFinal thresholds:\n- NT: n_kernel <= 150_000 AND m_kernel <= 2_000_000\n- B&B on subgraph: sub_n <= 500 AND time < 6 seconds\n\nHere\'s the final code:\n\nI\'m going to write it all in one clean pass now. Final decisions:\n- Use 150K/2M thresholds for NT\n- Use 500 for B&B subgraph size (within NT)\n- Use 8.5 seconds total time limit\n- Include two_one_swap for both NT fallback and large graph paths\n\nWriting now:\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::io::{self, Read, Write, BufWriter};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nfn main() {\n    std::thread::Builder::new()\n        .stack_size(256 * 1024 * 1024)\n        .spawn(run)\n        .unwrap()\n        .join()\n        .unwrap();\n}\n\nfn run() {\n    let start = Instant::now();\n    let stdout = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = BufWriter::new(stdout.lock());\n    \n    let mut input = String::new();\n    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut input).unwrap();\n    let mut it = input.split_ascii_whitespace();\n    macro_rules! rd { () => { it.next().unwrap().parse::<usize>().unwrap() }; }\n    \n    let n = rd!();\n    let m_raw = rd!();\n    \n    let mut edges: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::with_capacity(m_raw);\n    for _ in 0..m_raw {\n        let u = rd!();\n        let v = rd!();\n        if u != v { edges.push((u.min(v), u.max(v))); }\n    }\n    edges.sort_unstable();\n    edges.dedup();\n    \n    if n == 0 {\n        writeln!(out, "0").unwrap();\n        writeln!(out, "").unwrap();\n        return;\n    }\n    \n    let mut adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n];\n    for &(u, v) in &edges {\n        adj[u].push(v);\n        adj[v].push(u);\n    }\n    drop(edges);\n    \n    let mut active = vec![true; n];\n    let mut deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|i| adj[i].len()).collect();\n    let mut cov = vec![false; n];\n    \n    kernelize(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut deg, &mut cov);\n    \n    let nk: usize = active.iter().filter(|&&a| a).count();\n    let mk: usize = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).map(|v| deg[v]).sum::<usize>() / 2;\n    \n    if nk > 0 {\n        if nk <= 150_000 && mk <= 2_000_000 {\n            solve_nt(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut cov, &start);\n        } else {\n            greedy_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cov);\n            redux_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cov);\n            while start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                if !swap21_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cov) { break; }\n                redux_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cov);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let cover: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&i| cov[i]).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", cover.len()).unwrap();\n    let parts: Vec<String> = cover.iter().map(|x| x.to_string()).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", parts.join(" ")).unwrap();\n}\n\nfn kernelize(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n             deg: &mut Vec<usize>, cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut q: VecDeque<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| deg[v] <= 1).collect();\n    while let Some(v) = q.pop_front() {\n        if !active[v] { continue; }\n        if deg[v] == 0 {\n            active[v] = false;\n        } else {\n            match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied() {\n                None => { active[v] = false; }\n                Some(u) => {\n                    cov[u] = true; active[u] = false; active[v] = false;\n                    for &w in &adj[u] {\n                        if active[w] { deg[w] -= 1; if deg[w] <= 1 { q.push_back(w); } }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn solve_nt(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n            cov: &mut Vec<bool>, start: &Instant) {\n    let av: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).collect();\n    let na = av.len();\n    if na == 0 { return; }\n    let mut idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in av.iter().enumerate() { idx[v] = i; }\n    \n    let mut bi: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; na];\n    for &v in &av {\n        let vi = idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if active[u] { bi[vi].push(idx[u]); }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let (ml, mr) = hopcroft_karp(&bi, na, na);\n    let (cl, cr) = konig_cover(&bi, na, na, &ml, &mr);\n    \n    let mut xh: Vec<usize> = vec![];\n    for (i, &v) in av.iter().enumerate() {\n        match (cl[i], cr[i]) {\n            (true, true) => { cov[v] = true; active[v] = false; }\n            (false, false) => { active[v] = false; }\n            _ => { xh.push(v); }\n        }\n    }\n    if xh.is_empty() { return; }\n    \n    let sn = xh.len();\n    let mut si = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in xh.iter().enumerate() { si[v] = i; }\n    let mut sa: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; sn];\n    for &v in &xh {\n        let vi = si[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if si[u] != usize::MAX { sa[vi].push(si[u]); }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    let sc = if sn <= 500 && start.elapsed().as_millis() < 6000 {\n        bb_solve(sn, &sa, start)\n    } else {\n        let mut s = vec![false; sn];\n        greedy_vc(sn, &sa, &mut s);\n        redux(sn, &sa, &mut s);\n        while start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n            if !swap21(sn, &sa, &mut s) { break; }\n            redux(sn, &sa, &mut s);\n        }\n        s\n    };\n    \n    for (i, &inc) in sc.iter().enumerate() {\n        if inc { cov[xh[i]] = true; }\n    }\n}\n\nfn hopcroft_karp(adj: &[Vec<usize>], nl: usize, nr: usize) -> (Vec<usize>, Vec<usize>) {\n    let nil = nl;\n    let mut ml = vec![usize::MAX; nl];\n    let mut mr = vec![usize::MAX; nr];\n    let mut dist = vec![u32::MAX; nl + 1];\n    loop {\n        let mut q = VecDeque::new();\n        for u in 0..nl {\n            if ml[u] == usize::MAX { dist[u] = 0; q.push_back(u); }\n            else { dist[u] = u32::MAX; }\n        }\n        dist[nil] = u32::MAX;\n        while let Some(u) = q.pop_front() {\n            if dist[u] < dist[nil] {\n                for &v in &adj[u] {\n                    let w = if mr[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { mr[v] };\n                    if dist[w] == u32::MAX { dist[w] = dist[u] + 1; if w != nil { q.push_back(w); } }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        if dist[nil] == u32::MAX { break; }\n        let mut work = vec![0usize; nl];\n        for u in 0..nl {\n            if ml[u] == usize::MAX { dfs_hk(u, adj, &mut ml, &mut mr, &mut dist, &mut work, nil); }\n        }\n    }\n    (ml, mr)\n}\n\nfn dfs_hk(u: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], ml: &mut [usize], mr: &mut [usize],\n          dist: &mut [u32], work: &mut [usize], nil: usize) -> bool {\n    if u == nil { return true; }\n    while work[u] < adj[u].len() {\n        let v = adj[u][work[u]];\n        let w = if mr[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { mr[v] };\n        if dist[w] == dist[u] + 1 && dfs_hk(w, adj, ml, mr, dist, work, nil) {\n            mr[v] = u; ml[u] = v; return true;\n        }\n        work[u] += 1;\n    }\n    dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n    false\n}\n\nfn konig_cover(adj: &[Vec<usize>], nl: usize, nr: usize,\n               ml: &[usize], mr: &[usize]) -> (Vec<bool>, Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut zl = vec![false; nl];\n    let mut zr = vec![false; nr];\n    let mut q = VecDeque::new();\n    for u in 0..nl { if ml[u] == usize::MAX { zl[u] = true; q.push_back(u); } }\n    while let Some(u) = q.pop_front() {\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !zr[v] {\n                zr[v] = true;\n                if mr[v] != usize::MAX && !zl[mr[v]] { zl[mr[v]] = true; q.push_back(mr[v]); }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    ((0..nl).map(|u| !zl[u]).collect(), (0..nr).map(|v| zr[v]).collect())\n}\n\nfn bb_solve(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], start: &Instant) -> Vec<bool> {\n    let mut best = vec![false; n];\n    greedy_vc(n, adj, &mut best);\n    redux(n, adj, &mut best);\n    let mut bs = best.iter().filter(|&&b| b).count();\n    bb_rec(n, adj, vec![true; n], (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect(),\n           vec![false; n], 0, &mut bs, &mut best, start);\n    best\n}\n\nfn bb_rec(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n          mut act: Vec<bool>, mut deg: Vec<usize>, mut cov: Vec<bool>,\n          cur: usize, bsz: &mut usize, best: &mut Vec<bool>, start: &Instant) {\n    if start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8500 { return; }\n    let mut ex = 0usize;\n    let mut ch = true;\n    while ch {\n        ch = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if !act[v] { continue; }\n            if deg[v] == 0 { act[v] = false; ch = true; }\n            else if deg[v] == 1 {\n                match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| act[u]).copied() {\n                    None => { act[v] = false; ch = true; }\n                    Some(u) => {\n                        cov[u] = true; ex += 1; act[u] = false; act[v] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] { if act[w] { deg[w] -= 1; } }\n                        ch = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        let budget = bsz.saturating_sub(cur + ex + 1);\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if act[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n                cov[v] = true; ex += 1; act[v] = false;\n                for &w in &adj[v] { if act[w] { deg[w] -= 1; } }\n                ch = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    let nsz = cur + ex;\n    if nsz >= *bsz { return; }\n    let lb = glb(n, adj, &act);\n    if nsz + lb >= *bsz { return; }\n    let vopt = (0..n).filter(|&v| act[v] && deg[v] > 0).max_by_key(|&v| deg[v]);\n    match vopt {\n        None => { *bsz = nsz; *best = cov; }\n        Some(v) => {\n            { // Include v\n                let mut na = act.clone(); let mut nd = deg.clone(); let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                nc[v] = true; na[v] = false;\n                for &u in &adj[v] { if na[u] { nd[u] -= 1; } }\n                bb_rec(n, adj, na, nd, nc, nsz+1, bsz, best, start);\n            }\n            if start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                let nbrs: Vec<usize> = adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| act[u]).cloned().collect();\n                let k = nbrs.len();\n                if nsz + k < *bsz { // Exclude v\n                    let mut na = act.clone(); let mut nd = deg.clone(); let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                    na[v] = false;\n                    for &u in &nbrs {\n                        nc[u] = true; na[u] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] { if na[w] { nd[w] -= 1; } }\n                    }\n                    bb_rec(n, adj, na, nd, nc, nsz+k, bsz, best, start);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn glb(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], act: &[bool]) -> usize {\n    let mut m = vec![false; n]; let mut c = 0;\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if act[u] && !m[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if act[v] && !m[v] { m[u] = true; m[v] = true; c += 1; break; }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    c\n}\n\nfn greedy_vc(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cov[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] { if !cov[v] { cov[u] = true; cov[v] = true; break; } }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn redux(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut ch = true;\n    while ch { ch = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if cov[v] && adj[v].iter().all(|&u| cov[u]) { cov[v] = false; ch = true; }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], act: &[bool], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if act[u] && !cov[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] { if act[v] && !cov[v] { cov[u] = true; cov[v] = true; break; } }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn redux_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], act: &[bool], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut ch = true;\n    while ch { ch = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if act[v] && cov[v] && adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| act[u]).all(|&u| cov[u]) {\n                cov[v] = false; ch = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn swap21(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut uw: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cov[u] { continue; }\n        let mut cnt = 0; let mut w = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] { if !cov[v] { cnt += 1; w = v; if cnt > 1 { break; } } }\n        if cnt == 1 { uw[u] = w; }\n    }\n    let mut wf: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut ws: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if uw[u] != usize::MAX {\n            let w = uw[u];\n            if wf[w] == usize::MAX { wf[w] = u; } else if ws[w] == usize::MAX { ws[w] = u; }\n        }\n    }\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if !cov[w] && ws[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cov[wf[w]] = false; cov[ws[w]] = false; cov[w] = true; return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n\nfn swap21_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], act: &[bool], cov: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut uw: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !act[u] || !cov[u] { continue; }\n        let mut cnt = 0; let mut w = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] { if act[v] && !cov[v] { cnt += 1; w = v; if cnt > 1 { break; } } }\n        if cnt == 1 { uw[u] = w; }\n    }\n    let mut wf: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut ws: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if uw[u] != usize::MAX {\n            let w = uw[u];\n            if wf[w] == usize::MAX { wf[w] = u; } else if ws[w] == usize::MAX { ws[w] = u; }\n        }\n    }\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if act[w] && !cov[w] && ws[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cov[wf[w]] = false; cov[ws[w]] = false; cov[w] = true; return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n```\n\nThis looks complete. Let me check for any issues:\n\n1. In `run()`: `m_raw` is used for `Vec::with_capacity(m_raw)` and then the loop. But the actual used m (after dedup) is `edges.len()`. The `m_raw` variable is only needed for the `with_capacity` hint. Rust won\'t warn about `m_raw` being "unused" since it IS used (in the capacity and the loop count). ✓\n\nActually wait: after the loop, I don\'t use `m_raw` again. But I DO use it in the loop (`for _ in 0..m_raw`). So it\'s used. ✓\n\n2. In `konig_cover`, `nl` is used to create `zl` and iterate `0..nl`. `nr` is used to create `zr` and iterate `0..nr`. ✓\n\n3. In `dfs_hk`, the function name starts with `dfs_` which is fine. ✓\n\n4. In `solve_nt`, I use `si[u] != usize::MAX` to check if u is in the x=1/2 subgraph. But what if u is inactive (i.e., u was classified as x=0 or x=1)? Let me check: after the NT classification loop, we set `active[v] = false` for x=0 and x=1 vertices, but `si[u] != usize::MAX` only if u is in `xh` (x=1/2 vertices). Since active vertices that are not x=1/2 are deactivated, and adj[v] contains original neighbors (which might be inactive), we need to check: for active x=1/2 vertex v, its active neighbors are ONLY other x=1/2 vertices (no edges between x=0 and x=1/2 in the LP). But in the code, we don\'t check `active[u]` in the sub-adj construction:\n\n```rust\nfor &v in &xh {\n    let vi = si[v];\n    for &u in &adj[v] {\n        if si[u] != usize::MAX { sa[vi].push(si[u]); }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nHere, `si[u] != usize::MAX` means u is in x=1/2. So we only add edges to x=1/2 neighbors. This is correct even if u is an x=1 or x=0 vertex (those would have `si[u] = usize::MAX` and be skipped). ✓\n\nBut wait: could a x=1/2 vertex v have a neighbor u that is x=1 or x=0 in the original graph but NOT in the active set? Yes! After NT classification:\n- x=1 vertices: in cover, deactivated (`active[v] = false`)\n- x=0 vertices: not in cover, deactivated (`active[v] = false`)\n- x=1/2 vertices: still in xh, si[v] = their index\n\nFor a x=1/2 vertex v with a neighbor u that\'s x=1: the edge (v, u) is covered by u (which is in cover). So we don\'t add this edge to sa. ✓\n\nFor a x=1/2 vertex v with a neighbor u that\'s x=0: in the LP, this would violate the constraint x_v + x_u = 1/2 + 0 = 1/2 < 1. So this CAN\'T happen in a valid LP solution. ✓\n\nSo `si[u] != usize::MAX` correctly filters to only x=1/2 neighbors. ✓\n\n5. Memory usage for large n: For n=2M:\n- `adj`: up to 15M * 2 entries = 30M usize = 240MB. Hmm, 30M * 8 bytes = 240MB. Combined with other allocations:\n  - `active`: 2M bools = 2MB\n  - `deg`: 2M usize = 16MB\n  - `cov`: 2M bools = 2MB\n  - Input: ~240MB (15M edges * 16 bytes avg)\n  - `edges`: 15M * 16 bytes = 240MB (after dedup, might be less)\n  - Total: ~740MB. Well within 128GB. ✓\n\nActually, the adj vector itself: for n=2M vertices, the Vec<Vec<usize>> has 2M Vec headers = 2M * 24 bytes = 48MB. The total edge data: 30M * 8 bytes = 240MB. So adj total = 288MB. Fine.\n\n6. For the large graph case (greedy + swaps), the `swap21_active` function allocates `uw`, `wf`, `ws` arrays of size n=2M: 3 * 2M * 8 bytes = 48MB per call. With multiple calls in a loop, this is 48MB * num_iterations. But each Vec is allocated and freed each call. GC pressure could be an issue.\n\nTo optimize, I could pre-allocate these arrays and reuse them. But for simplicity, let me keep the current approach and hope the allocator is efficient.\n\nAlternatively, I can preallocate them once and pass them as mutable references. But that complicates the interface.\n\nFor now, let\'s keep it as-is. If performance is an issue, I can optimize later.\n\n7. In `bb_rec`, the high-degree rule loop:\n```rust\nfor v in 0..n {\n    if act[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n        ...\n        ch = true;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis sets `ch = true` inside the for loop, so the outer `while ch` loop will iterate again. But `budget` is computed before the for loop and might be stale (too large) as `ex` increases inside the loop. This means we might not apply the high-degree rule to some vertices in this iteration. The next outer loop iteration will fix this. ✓ (Correctness is maintained; efficiency might be slightly reduced.)\n\nTo improve efficiency, I could recompute budget inside the for loop:\n```rust\nlet budget = bsz.saturating_sub(cur + ex + 1);\n```\nBut this adds overhead. For small n (<=500), it\'s not critical.\n\nOK I think the code is complete and correct. Let me also think about edge cases:\n\n**Edge case: disconnected graph**\nThe algorithm handles this naturally since it processes all vertices. ✓\n\n**Edge case: complete graph Kn**\n- For small n: B&B finds optimal cover of size n-1 (all but one vertex)\n- For large n: greedy gives 2*(n-1)/2 = n-1 = OPT. Redundancy removal might give OPT.\n\n**Edge case: bipartite graph**\n- NT theorem should classify all vertices as x=0 or x=1 (no x=1/2)\n- Actually, for bipartite graphs, the LP is integral, so min |VC| = max matching\n- Hopcroft-Karp gives max matching, König\'s gives min VC\n- After NT, x=1/2 subgraph should be empty\n\nLet me verify: for a bipartite graph L∪R with a perfect matching M:\n- Bipartite doubling: L_left ∪ R_left ∪ L_right ∪ R_right (4 groups)\n- Edges: for each original edge (l, r): (l_left, r_right) and (r_left, l_right)\n- Actually, bi_adj only has left and right sides, each of size n.\n- For bipartite graph with L={0,...,k-1} and R={k,...,n-1}:\n  - Edges from l∈L to r∈R: bi_adj[l].push(r) and bi_adj[r].push(l)\n  - So bi_adj is symmetric.\n\nFor a bipartite graph, the doubled bipartite graph has a specific structure. The min VC of the doubled graph = 2 * OPT_LP = 2 * OPT_VC (for bipartite, LP=integer optimal). So the NT theorem gives x_v = 1 for v∈L in min VC and x_v = 0 for v∈R in min VC (or vice versa, depending on which side the König\'s algorithm chooses). This means all vertices are classified as x=0 or x=1, with none as x=1/2. ✓\n\n(Actually, the min VC of the original bipartite graph might not be just one side; it\'s determined by König\'s theorem. But the point is that for bipartite graphs, there\'s no x=1/2 subproblem.)\n\n**Edge case: cycle of odd length (triangle is a special case)**\n- Triangle: we showed all vertices are x=1/2\n- B&B solves this to size 2 ✓\n\n**Edge case: multiple connected components, some solvable by kernelization**\n- Kernelization handles each component independently ✓\n- NT theorem handles the remaining kernel ✓\n\nI think the algorithm is robust. Let me finalize.\n\nOne more thing: I should validate the final solution to ensure all edges are covered. But this would require O(m) time, which is fine. However, if there\'s a bug, this validation would catch it. For a production submission, I could include it as a non-fatal check that outputs a warning to stderr if validation fails.\n\nBut for now, let me omit it to keep the code clean.\n\nHere\'s the final code I\'ll submit. Let me clean it up one more time:\n\nActually, let me reconsider the B&B threshold. With `sub_n <= 500` and the B&B, could the B&B be too slow for some inputs?\n\nFor a random 3-regular graph on 500 vertices, the optimal VC is roughly (1 - 1/sqrt(2)) * n ≈ 146 vertices. The greedy gives ~200 vertices (2/3 * n ≈ 167 for random regular). The B&B with this initial bound needs to explore B&B tree of depth up to 146.\n\nWith the LP lower bound (greedy matching gives n/2 = 250 for 3-regular), and initial bound of 200, we\'d be searching for covers of size ≤ 200. The search space could be large.\n\nFor very hard instances, the B&B might timeout. The time check `start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8500` would stop it and return the best-found (which might not be optimal but is valid).\n\nLet me also add the greedy + swap solution as a safety net: before running B&B, compute greedy + swap solution, and if B&B times out, the greedy + swap solution is still returned.\n\nThis is already done in `bb_solve`: the initial `best` is the greedy solution, and B&B only updates it when it finds something better. So if B&B times out, we return the greedy solution. ✓\n\nBut for the subproblem in `solve_nt`, the greedy + swap is used as the fallback when `sub_n > 500`. For `sub_n <= 500`, we run B&B which might timeout and return the greedy solution. ✓\n\nAlright, the code handles timeouts gracefully. ✓\n\nNow, let me check one more potential issue: `sub_n` is the number of x=1/2 vertices. For the B&B on the subgraph, the initial greedy + redundancy removal gives a solution of size ≤ sub_n. The B&B tries to improve. If sub_n is 500 and the optimal is, say, 250, the B&B needs to explore a large search space. With 6 seconds budget (start.elapsed() < 6000ms), and the B&B checking time every node, it should be manageable for most practical instances.\n\nFor pathological instances (where B&B is genuinely exponential), the time limit kicks in and we return the greedy solution.\n\nOK I\'m satisfied with the design. Final code:\n\nActually, I want to also double-check the output format. I\'ll spend 10 minutes on this and not second-guess anymore.\n\nFinal note on potential issue: In the bb_rec, when I set cov[v] = true (include v in branch 1) and nc[v] is true in the clone `nc`, the `nc[v] = true` line is explicit. Just making sure the logic is correct.\n\nOK writing the code NOW:\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::io::{self, Read, Write, BufWriter};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nfn main() {\n    std::thread::Builder::new()\n        .stack_size(256 * 1024 * 1024)\n        .spawn(run)\n        .unwrap()\n        .join()\n        .unwrap();\n}\n\nfn run() {\n    let start = Instant::now();\n    let stdout = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = BufWriter::new(stdout.lock());\n\n    let mut input = String::new();\n    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut input).unwrap();\n    let mut it = input.split_ascii_whitespace();\n\n    macro_rules! parse {\n        () => { it.next().unwrap().parse::<usize>().unwrap() };\n    }\n\n    let n = parse!();\n    let m_hint = parse!();\n\n    let mut edges: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::with_capacity(m_hint);\n    for _ in 0..m_hint {\n        let u = parse!();\n        let v = parse!();\n        if u != v {\n            edges.push((u.min(v), u.max(v)));\n        }\n    }\n    edges.sort_unstable();\n    edges.dedup();\n\n    if n == 0 {\n        writeln!(out, "0").unwrap();\n        writeln!(out, "").unwrap();\n        return;\n    }\n\n    let mut adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; n];\n    for &(u, v) in &edges {\n        adj[u].push(v);\n        adj[v].push(u);\n    }\n    drop(edges);\n\n    let mut active = vec![true; n];\n    let mut deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|i| adj[i].len()).collect();\n    let mut cover = vec![false; n];\n\n    // Phase 1: Kernelization (degree-0 and degree-1 reduction)\n    kernelize(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut deg, &mut cover);\n\n    let n_kernel: usize = active.iter().filter(|&&a| a).count();\n    let m_kernel: usize = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).map(|v| deg[v]).sum::<usize>() / 2;\n\n    if n_kernel > 0 {\n        if n_kernel <= 150_000 && m_kernel <= 2_000_000 {\n            // Phase 2a: NT theorem + exact or greedy on subproblem\n            solve_nt(n, &adj, &mut active, &mut cover, &start);\n        } else {\n            // Phase 2b: Greedy approximation + local search\n            greedy_on_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cover);\n            remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cover);\n            while start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                if !swap21_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cover) {\n                    break;\n                }\n                remove_redundant_active(n, &adj, &active, &mut cover);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Output\n    let result: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&i| cover[i]).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", result.len()).unwrap();\n    let parts: Vec<String> = result.iter().map(|x| x.to_string()).collect();\n    writeln!(out, "{}", parts.join(" ")).unwrap();\n}\n\n// Kernelization: repeatedly remove degree-0 vertices and apply degree-1 rule\nfn kernelize(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    deg: &mut Vec<usize>,\n    cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut queue: VecDeque<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| deg[v] <= 1).collect();\n    while let Some(v) = queue.pop_front() {\n        if !active[v] {\n            continue;\n        }\n        if deg[v] == 0 {\n            active[v] = false;\n        } else {\n            // deg[v] == 1 (since active and deg was <= 1 when enqueued, can only have decreased)\n            match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| active[u]).copied() {\n                None => {\n                    active[v] = false;\n                }\n                Some(u) => {\n                    cover[u] = true;\n                    active[u] = false;\n                    active[v] = false;\n                    for &w in &adj[u] {\n                        if active[w] {\n                            deg[w] -= 1;\n                            if deg[w] <= 1 {\n                                queue.push_back(w);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// NT theorem: apply Nemhauser-Trotter theorem to classify vertices\nfn solve_nt(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    let active_verts: Vec<usize> = (0..n).filter(|&v| active[v]).collect();\n    let na = active_verts.len();\n    if na == 0 {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    let mut to_idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in active_verts.iter().enumerate() {\n        to_idx[v] = i;\n    }\n\n    // Build doubled bipartite graph\n    // Left vertex i = active_verts[i]_L, Right vertex i = active_verts[i]_R\n    // For each original edge (v, u): add (v_L -> u_R) and (u_L -> v_R)\n    let mut bi_adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; na];\n    for &v in &active_verts {\n        let vi = to_idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if active[u] {\n                bi_adj[vi].push(to_idx[u]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Find max matching in doubled bipartite graph\n    let (match_l, match_r) = hopcroft_karp(&bi_adj, na, na);\n\n    // Find min vertex cover via König\'s theorem\n    let (cover_l, cover_r) = konig_cover(&bi_adj, na, na, &match_l, &match_r);\n\n    // Classify vertices:\n    // cover_l[i] & cover_r[i] = true => x=1 (must be in VC)\n    // cover_l[i] = cover_r[i] = false => x=0 (not in VC)\n    // otherwise => x=1/2 (undecided)\n    let mut x_half: Vec<usize> = vec![];\n    for (i, &v) in active_verts.iter().enumerate() {\n        match (cover_l[i], cover_r[i]) {\n            (true, true) => {\n                cover[v] = true;\n                active[v] = false;\n            }\n            (false, false) => {\n                active[v] = false;\n            }\n            _ => {\n                x_half.push(v);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    if x_half.is_empty() {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    let sub_n = x_half.len();\n    let mut sub_idx = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for (i, &v) in x_half.iter().enumerate() {\n        sub_idx[v] = i;\n    }\n\n    // Build subgraph on x=1/2 vertices\n    let mut sub_adj: Vec<Vec<usize>> = vec![vec![]; sub_n];\n    for &v in &x_half {\n        let vi = sub_idx[v];\n        for &u in &adj[v] {\n            if sub_idx[u] != usize::MAX {\n                sub_adj[vi].push(sub_idx[u]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Solve subproblem\n    let sub_cover = if sub_n <= 500 && start.elapsed().as_millis() < 6000 {\n        bb_solve(sub_n, &sub_adj, start)\n    } else {\n        let mut sc = vec![false; sub_n];\n        greedy_vc(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        remove_redundant(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        while start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n            if !swap21(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc) {\n                break;\n            }\n            remove_redundant(sub_n, &sub_adj, &mut sc);\n        }\n        sc\n    };\n\n    for (i, &inc) in sub_cover.iter().enumerate() {\n        if inc {\n            cover[x_half[i]] = true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Hopcroft-Karp bipartite matching\nfn hopcroft_karp(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    n_left: usize,\n    n_right: usize,\n) -> (Vec<usize>, Vec<usize>) {\n    let nil = n_left;\n    let mut match_l = vec![usize::MAX; n_left];\n    let mut match_r = vec![usize::MAX; n_right];\n    let mut dist = vec![u32::MAX; n_left + 1];\n\n    loop {\n        // BFS phase\n        let mut queue = VecDeque::new();\n        for u in 0..n_left {\n            if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dist[u] = 0;\n                queue.push_back(u);\n            } else {\n                dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n            }\n        }\n        dist[nil] = u32::MAX;\n\n        while let Some(u) = queue.pop_front() {\n            if dist[u] < dist[nil] {\n                for &v in &adj[u] {\n                    let w = if match_r[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { match_r[v] };\n                    if dist[w] == u32::MAX {\n                        dist[w] = dist[u] + 1;\n                        if w != nil {\n                            queue.push_back(w);\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if dist[nil] == u32::MAX {\n            break;\n        }\n\n        // DFS phase\n        let mut work = vec![0usize; n_left];\n        for u in 0..n_left {\n            if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n                dfs_hk(u, adj, &mut match_l, &mut match_r, &mut dist, &mut work, nil);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    (match_l, match_r)\n}\n\nfn dfs_hk(\n    u: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    match_l: &mut [usize],\n    match_r: &mut [usize],\n    dist: &mut [u32],\n    work: &mut [usize],\n    nil: usize,\n) -> bool {\n    if u == nil {\n        return true;\n    }\n    while work[u] < adj[u].len() {\n        let v = adj[u][work[u]];\n        let w = if match_r[v] == usize::MAX { nil } else { match_r[v] };\n        if dist[w] == dist[u] + 1 && dfs_hk(w, adj, match_l, match_r, dist, work, nil) {\n            match_r[v] = u;\n            match_l[u] = v;\n            return true;\n        }\n        work[u] += 1;\n    }\n    dist[u] = u32::MAX;\n    false\n}\n\n// König\'s theorem: min vertex cover from max matching\nfn konig_cover(\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    n_left: usize,\n    n_right: usize,\n    match_l: &[usize],\n    match_r: &[usize],\n) -> (Vec<bool>, Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut in_z_l = vec![false; n_left];\n    let mut in_z_r = vec![false; n_right];\n    let mut queue = VecDeque::new();\n\n    // Z starts from unmatched left vertices\n    for u in 0..n_left {\n        if match_l[u] == usize::MAX {\n            in_z_l[u] = true;\n            queue.push_back(u);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Alternating BFS\n    while let Some(u) = queue.pop_front() {\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !in_z_r[v] {\n                in_z_r[v] = true;\n                if match_r[v] != usize::MAX && !in_z_l[match_r[v]] {\n                    in_z_l[match_r[v]] = true;\n                    queue.push_back(match_r[v]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Cover = (L \\ Z_L) ∪ (R ∩ Z_R)\n    let cover_l: Vec<bool> = (0..n_left).map(|u| !in_z_l[u]).collect();\n    let cover_r: Vec<bool> = (0..n_right).map(|v| in_z_r[v]).collect();\n    (cover_l, cover_r)\n}\n\n// Exact branch and bound for small graphs\nfn bb_solve(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], start: &Instant) -> Vec<bool> {\n    let mut best = vec![false; n];\n    greedy_vc(n, adj, &mut best);\n    remove_redundant(n, adj, &mut best);\n    let mut best_size = best.iter().filter(|&&b| b).count();\n\n    let init_active = vec![true; n];\n    let init_deg: Vec<usize> = (0..n).map(|v| adj[v].len()).collect();\n    let init_cov = vec![false; n];\n\n    bb_recurse(\n        n, adj, init_active, init_deg, init_cov, 0,\n        &mut best_size, &mut best, start,\n    );\n    best\n}\n\nfn bb_recurse(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    mut act: Vec<bool>,\n    mut deg: Vec<usize>,\n    mut cov: Vec<bool>,\n    cur_size: usize,\n    best_size: &mut usize,\n    best: &mut Vec<bool>,\n    start: &Instant,\n) {\n    if start.elapsed().as_millis() > 8500 {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Apply reduction rules\n    let mut extra = 0usize;\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n\n        // Rule 1: remove isolated vertices\n        // Rule 2: degree-1 rule\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if !act[v] {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if deg[v] == 0 {\n                act[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            } else if deg[v] == 1 {\n                match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| act[u]).copied() {\n                    None => {\n                        act[v] = false;\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                    Some(u) => {\n                        cov[u] = true;\n                        extra += 1;\n                        act[u] = false;\n                        act[v] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if act[w] {\n                                deg[w] -= 1;\n                            }\n                        }\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Rule 3: high-degree rule\n        let budget = best_size.saturating_sub(cur_size + extra + 1);\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if act[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n                cov[v] = true;\n                extra += 1;\n                act[v] = false;\n                for &w in &adj[v] {\n                    if act[w] {\n                        deg[w] -= 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    let new_size = cur_size + extra;\n\n    // Prune by size\n    if new_size >= *best_size {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Prune by lower bound (greedy matching)\n    let lb = greedy_matching_lb(n, adj, &act);\n    if new_size + lb >= *best_size {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Find max-degree active vertex with edges\n    let v_opt = (0..n)\n        .filter(|&v| act[v] && deg[v] > 0)\n        .max_by_key(|&v| deg[v]);\n\n    match v_opt {\n        None => {\n            // All active vertices are isolated: cover is complete\n            *best_size = new_size;\n            *best = cov;\n        }\n        Some(v) => {\n            // Branch 1: include v\n            {\n                let mut na = act.clone();\n                let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                nc[v] = true;\n                na[v] = false;\n                for &u in &adj[v] {\n                    if na[u] {\n                        nd[u] -= 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + 1, best_size, best, start);\n            }\n\n            // Branch 2: exclude v (include all active neighbors)\n            if start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                let neighbors: Vec<usize> = adj[v]\n                    .iter()\n                    .filter(|&&u| act[u])\n                    .cloned()\n                    .collect();\n                let k = neighbors.len();\n                if new_size + k < *best_size {\n                    let mut na = act.clone();\n                    let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                    let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                    na[v] = false; // exclude v\n                    for &u in &neighbors {\n                        nc[u] = true;\n                        na[u] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if na[w] {\n                                nd[w] -= 1;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + k, best_size, best, start);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_matching_lb(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool]) -> usize {\n    let mut matched = vec![false; n];\n    let mut count = 0;\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !matched[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !matched[v] {\n                    matched[u] = true;\n                    matched[v] = true;\n                    count += 1;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    count\n}\n\nfn greedy_vc(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if !cover[v] {\n                    cover[u] = true;\n                    cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if cover[v] && adj[v].iter().all(|&u| cover[u]) {\n                cover[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_on_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !cover[v] {\n                    cover[u] = true;\n                    cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant_active(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &[bool],\n    cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && cover[v] {\n                if adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| active[u]).all(|&u| cover[u]) {\n                    cover[v] = false;\n                    changed = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// 2-1 swap for subgraph (all vertices active)\nfn swap21(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut unique_w: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n]; // unique non-cover neighbor\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cover[u] {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let mut cnt = 0;\n        let mut w_found = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !cover[v] {\n                cnt += 1;\n                w_found = v;\n                if cnt > 1 {\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 {\n            unique_w[u] = w_found;\n        }\n    }\n\n    let mut w_first: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut w_second: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if unique_w[u] != usize::MAX {\n            let w = unique_w[u];\n            if w_first[w] == usize::MAX {\n                w_first[w] = u;\n            } else if w_second[w] == usize::MAX {\n                w_second[w] = u;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if !cover[w] && w_second[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cover[w_first[w]] = false;\n            cover[w_second[w]] = false;\n            cover[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n\n// 2-1 swap for active subgraph\nfn swap21_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut unique_w: Vec<usize> = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !active[u] || !cover[u] {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let mut cnt = 0;\n        let mut w_found = 0;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if active[v] && !cover[v] {\n                cnt += 1;\n                w_found = v;\n                if cnt > 1 {\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 {\n            unique_w[u] = macro_rules! parse {\n        () => {\n            it.next().unwrap().parse::<usize>().unwrap()\n        };\n    }\n\n    let n = parse!();\n    let m_hint = parse!();\n\n    let mut edges:            match adj[v].iter().find(|&&u| act[u]).copied() {\n                    None => {\n                        act[v] = false;\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n              for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if act[w] {\n                                deg[w] -= 1;\n                            }\n                        }\n                        changed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        let budget = best_size.saturating_sub(cur_size + extra + 1);\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if act[v] && deg[v] > budget {\n                cov[v] = true;\n                extra += 1;\n                act[v] = false;\n                for &w in &adj[v] {\n                    if act[w] {\n                        deg[w] -= 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    let new_size = cur_size + extra;\n\n    if new_size >= *best_size {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    let lb = greedy_matching_lb(n, adj, &act);\n    if new_size + lb >= *best_size {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    let v_opt = (0..n)\n        .filter(|&v| act[v] && deg[v] > 0)\n        .max_by_key(|&v| deg[v]);\n\n    match v_opt {\n        None => {\n            *best_size = new_size;\n            *best = cov;\n        }\n        Some(v) => {\n            // Branch 1: include v\n            {\n                let mut na = act.clone();\n                let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                nc[v] = true;\n                na[v] = false;\n                for &u in &adj[v] {\n                    if na[u] {\n                        nd[u] -= 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + 1, best_size, best, start);\n            }\n\n            // Branch 2: exclude v, include all active neighbors\n            if start.elapsed().as_millis() < 8500 {\n                let neighbors: Vec<usize> =\n                    adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| act[u]).cloned().collect();\n                let k = neighbors.len();\n                if new_size + k < *best_size {\n                    let mut na = act.clone();\n                    let mut nd = deg.clone();\n                    let mut nc = cov.clone();\n                    na[v] = false;\n                    for &u in &neighbors {\n                        nc[u] = true;\n                        na[u] = false;\n                        for &w in &adj[u] {\n                            if na[w] {\n                                nd[w] -= 1;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    bb_recurse(n, adj, na, nd, nc, new_size + k, best_size, best, start);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_matching_lb(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool]) -> usize {\n    let mut matched = vec![false; n];\n    let mut count = 0;\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !matched[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !matched[v] {\n                    matched[u] = true;\n                    matched[v] = true;\n                    count += 1;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    count\n}\n\nfn greedy_vc(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if !cover[v] {\n                    cover[u] = true;\n                    cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if cover[v] && adj[v].iter().all(|&u| cover[u]) {\n                cover[v] = false;\n                changed = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn greedy_on_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) {\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if active[u] && !cover[u] {\n            for &v in &adj[u] {\n                if active[v] && !cover[v] {\n                    cover[u] = true;\n                    cover[v] = true;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn remove_redundant_active(\n    n: usize,\n    adj: &[Vec<usize>],\n    active: &[bool],\n    cover: &mut Vec<bool>,\n) {\n    let mut changed = true;\n    while changed {\n        changed = false;\n        for v in 0..n {\n            if active[v] && cover[v] {\n                if adj[v].iter().filter(|&&u| active[u]).all(|&u| cover[u]) {\n                    cover[v] = false;\n                    changed = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn swap21(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut unique_w = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !cover[u] {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let mut cnt = 0usize;\n        let mut w_found = 0usize;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if !cover[v] {\n                cnt += 1;\n                w_found = v;\n                if cnt > 1 {\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 {\n            unique_w[u] = w_found;\n        }\n    }\n\n    let mut w_first = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut w_second = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if unique_w[u] != usize::MAX {\n            let w = unique_w[u];\n            if w_first[w] == usize::MAX {\n                w_first[w] = u;\n            } else if w_second[w] == usize::MAX {\n                w_second[w] = u;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if !cover[w] && w_second[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cover[w_first[w]] = false;\n            cover[w_second[w]] = false;\n            cover[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n\nfn swap21_active(n: usize, adj: &[Vec<usize>], active: &[bool], cover: &mut Vec<bool>) -> bool {\n    let mut unique_w = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if !active[u] || !cover[u] {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let mut cnt = 0usize;\n        let mut w_found = 0usize;\n        for &v in &adj[u] {\n            if active[v] && !cover[v] {\n                cnt += 1;\n                w_found = v;\n                if cnt > 1 {\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        if cnt == 1 {\n            unique_w[u] = w_found;\n        }\n    }\n\n    let mut w_first = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    let mut w_second = vec![usize::MAX; n];\n    for u in 0..n {\n        if unique_w[u] != usize::MAX {\n            let w = unique_w[u];\n            if w_first[w] == usize::MAX {\n                w_first[w] = u;\n            } else if w_second[w] == usize::MAX {\n                w_second[w] = u;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    for w in 0..n {\n        if active[w] && !cover[w] && w_second[w] != usize::MAX {\n            cover[w_first[w]] = false;\n            cover[w_second[w]] = false;\n            cover[w] = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}'}
